<time>1545234777781< /time><Rate>5</Rate><text>Okay having been at this spot three times now I can give a high level overview of why I give this place five stars.

Parking: Self parking available across the street but offers well priced valet.

Location: Restaurant is located on the 72nd floor with amazing skyline views at every corner.

Food: Good food, not what I would consider great but almost there if it weren't for the high cost. I'm sure it's to pay the lease and overhead so overall fair enough food value.

Service: Great wait staff who always make you feel welcomed and are really enthusiastic about showcasing what the restaurant is all about. They make sure you are getting the most of the experience. They truly make you feel like a valued customer but also appreciate you picking them over other locations.

Overall because of the amazing views, parking and service I'm truly impressed and will continue to go so long as these points don't change, otherwise It would be a place I'd go to one a year and not once a month like I have been doing.</text><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPmJMbXsvaf865xHffyhROq1d9Kxk9fO6Jk_HGb=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPYU-_wWU4UkrrC9V802nl9Pjq41IQe5Jb4zt4n=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMrj_S5XHh6C0YV5x_4BI5gL-pT5NhMHMx5u7zL=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNr0UHmaJbrDMdv3DkPkdtzr9dZV8lS0dITGiEV=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics>< response>

<user_id>114432217686683066647<//user_id><Name>Carlie Guthrie<//Name>< time>
1572712787988<//time>
<Rate>2</Rate><Text>We decided to try this place for dineLA last Saturday. I snagged a sweet reservation at 7:45pm and requested a table by the window. We arrived early so the hostess had us wait in the bar. I was a bit annoyed that she didn't ask to take our coats as the chairs are not coat-friendly. We ordered a round of cocktails at the bar. The cocktails were beautifully presented and were great. After feeling awkward wearing my coat at the bar, I had my husband take our coats to the front desk where they finally checked our coats.

However, they were able to seat us early and even gave us a table by the window which we were really happy to get.

We did not like the amuse bouche - the potato really muted the taste of the caviar. The 1st course of the salad was ok, nothing special. The 2nd course - veal tartare was so soft and tender. We did not like the squab in the 3rd course. It had a strange texture and the taste was really bland. The 4th course of wagyu steak was amazing! And the last course - salted caramel chocolate tart was absolutely decadent. Out of the 6 courses, I would say that we only thoroughly enjoyed the wagyu steak and the dessert. Service between each course was painfully slow. The food simply was not up to par with our expectations. I also noticed that other customers who came in were not offered to check their coats in and were awkwardly stuffing them on their chair. The hostess really should offer the option of checking in their coats when they arrive. I see it offered constantly in the east coast and it should be offered here in the west coast as well. It's a nice gesture to customers who are paying for a fine dining experience.

In addition, previous helpers said valet was $11 with validation but we paid $28! I recommend going to the bar only for cocktails and the lovely view. The food here is totally overrated and lackluster.<//Text>< Pictures>

Before receiving our steaks we were offered to choose our steak knife from a selection from around the world. < name>

< GmapID>
0x80c2c7b110884f6d:0x41ee169e861331c4</GmapID>
< pics>
[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN5dpmIfHVj2eM35USiObuigPpKDnZUqMKb0BcM=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOEAO0wwP3p8sPQmXkQS4MFy7Hjcuvi4kIwCLKj=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNEpZyWBj_SOJwL7kwxsU94WjPNTkqSMVHgmAtp=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM4pBEwD3VfRWn9jbSOwNSQnStBuMtgMm-VKVAv=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNXkZkgR-VUFa1PBpMRKgQMNuES6OUquwvRlSOR=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOpTI0pYWgkVyJqXbTDidzS_JpBDA0Y6iGh4msW=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pics>
< Review>
Food - 3 * - The small plates were mostly good, so I give it 4*, but the steak is a 3* at best.  We ordered the Saumon, Foie Gras, Dungeness crab salad, and French onion soup.  The saumon with caviar, as well as the dungeness crab salad, was delicious and fresh!  Perhaps the Plateau de Fruits de Mer would have been the best option from the menu given the freshness of the seafood appetizers.  The Foie Gras was excellent too with the berry puff pastry, although I would say it's hard to go wrong as long as you buy top quality Foie and sear well.  Our waiter boasts that the french onion soup is cooked for 3 days before serving, so I had to give it a try.  It ended up being the most disappointing french onion soup I've ever had in my life.  It was overly sweet (is it supposed to be sweet? A first for me), and had a small slice of gruyere that was mediocre in flavor and wasn't even baked long enough for a nice burnt on top.

We ordered the 60 day dry aged ribeye and duck fat fries, which was highly recommended by the waiter and some of my friends.  The ribeye was okay.  Not bad, not great.  It was served in a warm plate, not hot like other high end steakhouses.  We ordered medium rare, but it was overcooked along a good portion of the outer parts.  Only about 50% of the steak was truly medium rare (the photo might deceive you).  You'd think the 60 day age should give it immense flavor, but it was disappointing.  In fact, the dry age ribeye at Fleming's and the (non-age) ribeye at Ruth Chris taste far far better, and at nearly half the price!  For a restaurant claimed to offer "premium world class steaks" that charge $95 for a 12oz ribeye, they did not live up to expectations.  The duck fat fries was also a let down.  Firstly, it was served warm, not hot out of the fryer.  I had a couple fries that had a hint of duck fat flavor, but the rest tasted just like regular potatoes with no duck flavor at all.  It didn't even taste like fries because it wasn't really crispy on the outside.  The potatoes were also dry on the inside.  You get better fries at other steak houses or even fast food restaurants than this place!

Service - 2* - Our waiter was a nice gentleman at the very beginning, but it went downhill after that.  Maybe because we didn't order alcohol?  I'm not sure.  We asked for water with some lemon, and ended up asking for lemons 3 times.  We ended up asking his assistant waiter 2 times and finally got our lemons.  We asked if they have any cocktail non-alcoholic drinks, and he said they didn't have any, but they can mix something up.  So we asked to make something like a strawberry daiquiri.  He said it should be no problem.  After a good 15 mins, we asked him again, and he said it's no problem and should be coming right up.  Asked second time, still waiting.  45mins later, we asked the 3rd time, and he forgot.  We told him to just cancel it.  After an hour into dining, we were still waiting for our soup.  Other parties who arrived later than us already finished their main entrees.  Was it a kitchen delay or service delay?  All I know is that the soup was not worth waiting an hour for.  If it was cooked for 3 days, do you really need to cook longer to serve it?  I would think it's readily available and the cheese should only take 5-10 mins to cook/baked to perfection.

Ambience - 2* - The view is definitely beautiful and probably one of the main reasons why people want to dine here, especially considering there aren't a lot of restaurants with a skyscraper view in LA.  However, downtown LA is not the most impressive to view compare to many other cities in the world, so don't have high hopes.  If you are looking for a quiet evening, you won't find it here unless you booked a private chef's table.  The main dining hall is very loud, and you could hear almost everyone's conversations around you.

I would definitely not come back again, nor would I recommend this place to anyone.  For the price we paid, we could have afford a much more elegant 8-10 course tasting from a high-end French restaurant.<//Review>

<rating>2</rating><review>We decided to try this place for dineLA last Saturday. I snagged a sweet reservation at 7:45pm and requested a table by the window. We arrived early so the hostess had us wait in the bar. I was a bit annoyed that she didn't ask to take our coats as the chairs are not coat-friendly. We ordered a round of cocktails at the bar. The cocktails were beautifully presented and were great. After feeling awkward wearing my coat at the bar, I had my husband take our coats to the front desk where they finally checked our coats.

However, they were able to seat us early and even gave us a table by the window which we were really happy to get.

We did not like the amuse bouche - the potato really muted the taste of the caviar. The 1st course of the salad was ok, nothing special. The 2nd course - veal tartare was so soft and tender. We did not like the squab in the 3rd course. It had a strange texture and the taste was really bland. The 4th course of wagyu steak was amazing! And the last course - salted caramel chocolate tart was absolutely decadent. Out of the 6 courses, I would say that we only thoroughly enjoyed the wagyu steak and the dessert. Service between each course was painfully slow. The food simply was not up to par with our expectations. I also noticed that other customers who came in were not offered to check their coats in and were awkwardly stuffing them on their chair. The hostess really should offer the option of checking in their coats when they arrive. I see it offered constantly in the east coast and it should be offered here in the west coast as well. It's a nice gesture to customers who are paying for a fine dining experience.

In addition, previous helpers said valet was $11 with validation but we paid $28! I recommend going to the bar only for cocktails and the lovely view. The food here is totally overrated and lackluster.< /review>< username>

<Name>Sara Klipps</Name><time>1566226629850</time><Rate>2</Rate>< Review>
We decided to try this place for dineLA last Saturday. I snagged a sweet reservation at 7:45pm and requested a table by the window. We arrived early so the hostess had us wait in the bar. I was a bit annoyed that she didn't ask to take our coats as the chairs are not coat-friendly. We ordered a round of cocktails at the bar. The cocktails were beautifully presented and were great. After feeling awkward wearing my coat at the bar, I had my husband take our coats to the front desk where they finally checked our coats.

However, they were able to seat us early and even gave us a table by the window which we were really happy to get.

We did not like the amuse bouche - the potato really muted the taste of the caviar. The 1st course of the salad was ok, nothing special. The 2nd course - veal tartare was so soft and tender. We did not like the squab in the 3rd course. It had a strange texture and the taste was really bland. The 4th course of wagyu steak was amazing! And the last course - salted caramel chocolate tart was absolutely decadent. Out of the 6 courses, I would say that we only thoroughly enjoyed the wagyu steak and the dessert. Service between each course was painfully slow. The food simply was not up to par with our expectations. I also noticed that other customers who came in were not offered to check their coats in and were awkwardly stuffing them on their chair. The hostess really should offer the option of checking in their coats when they arrive. I see it offered constantly in the east coast and it should be offered here in the west coast as well. It's a nice gesture to customers who are paying for a fine dining experience.

In addition, previous helpers said valet was $11 with validation but we paid $28! I recommend going to the bar only for cocktails and the lovely view. The food here is totally overrated and lackluster.<//Review>

Overall, the atmosphere was good, service was ok, and food was commendable. The views are worth it. Overlooking the city at sunset with city lights was beautiful. Had the filet and dry aged kansas strip. Filet was good quality and the kansas was well portioned. Had the filet and ahi tar tar and watermelon gazpacho for starters. Tar tar was wrapped  like cigars which was unique, but overall taste was mediocre. The accent flavors masked the taste of the beef tar tar. Service was solid, but for the level of dining, expected more. Compared to 71 above, service did not meet the standard 71 above set.< /Text>

< Review>
Favorite neighborhood spot to grab breakfast, lunch, or simply a quick bite!

Parking: side street parking only

Prices: Very decent!

Food: Croissant and bagel sandwiches galore! They also serve coffee.

Customer service: They are so nice and super helpful. Always has a smile on his face.

Tip: Because their bagels are house-made and super fresh (made on the same day you order), they are sold for $5 a pack the next day if you want to bring some bagels home with you!

Will I go back again: Yes! My boyfriend literally dreams of the ham and cheese croissant sandwich.</Review>

< review>
First of all, I wanna say that I really wanted to like this place. The atmosphere was good, and gave us the assumption that the pizza would be high quality. My girlfriend and I were immediately impressed. when we recieved our food, Togo, and went back to our room to enjoy. We loved the presentation and were visually impressed. This changed when we went to eat, first the crust was ridiculous, it was so thin there was no support for the toppings and everything fell off. We basically had to eat it with a fork, no big deal. We also ordered a Nutella calzone which we were eager to try. The first bite was meh, it was very Nutella tasting with some kind of tart sourish sauce to contrast the flavor. I noticed it was especially hard to cut so I checked the bottom after he first bite only to notice the bottom dough was entirely raw, to the point I could basically shape it if I wanted. This is horrendously undercooked. Not worth the 40 dollars I paid for 2 drinks, a mediocre pizza and an undercooked dessert.

<userid>102005300299674371869<//userid><Review>Very good pizza, not the best in Monterey, but very good. There are two parts of a great pizza: the ingredients and the way they go together. First, the ingredients. The crust was fresh, flavorful and slightly chewy. It was about 1/8 inch thick. I liked it, but if you prefer a crisp thin crust you will be disappointed. The tomato sauce was excellent! Very fresh and with a rich tomato flavor. The cheese was good, but was not fully melted and was lumpy. The basil was fresh. The prosciutto was excellent! Very rich and not too fatty. Now, the combination. The pizza needed a little more tomato sauce. The cheese was placed on the pizza in large lumps which did not melt. So some bites had no cheese at all and some tasted only of cheese. There was WAY too much basil. I removed about 1/2 cup and there was still plenty on the pizza. Some other reviews have mentioned that there was not enough basil. Now they have gone to the other extreme. The prosciutto was just right. Covered the entire pizza but was thinly sliced as it should be, so it was perfect.

Al in all, a very good, but not great pizza.<//Review><response>{'time': 1544808317489, 'text': "We love a thorough review, Richard. Hoping we'll have another chance to prove our pizza to be absolutely great soon! -Alma M., Owner"}< /response>< username>

<rate>2< /rate><review>I have been to this restaurant about 3 times in the past 5 months. 2 out of those 3 times I have been rather inconvenienced. My first experience was pleasant, no problems. The 2nd time, we waited about 30 minutes before we got our food. The waitress we had seemed a little overwhelmed and she appeared to be the only one running food, which I wouldn't consider to be very efficient. I don't place any blame on her performance, and on that count she had brought us food that we did not order so we had to wait to have our food remade. This past time, I had to wait almost 40 minutes to get my food. I placed my order at about 6:15 and while waiting I got caught up in conversation. I checked the clock later on and about 25 minutes had passed and I realized I was the only person who hadn't received their food. So I got up and asked where the cooks were in the process with my food, and the response I got was "oh, we'll get started on that right away". 25 minutes....and my food hadn't even been started. I think I'm correct in assuming they had completely forgotten about my order. To note, from the amount of customers inside this entire time, they were not busy at all. An experience that started out unpleasant and continued to get worse. Ordering at the crowded counter with a long line and only one cashier took about 20 minutes. When I asked what was the soup of the day, it took 3 people to finally get the answer. I ordered the meatballs, which are noted on the menu to the a "favorite" and tomato soup for myself and a panini for my husband. My order came out quickly in about 10 min. However, my soup was cold and looked/tasted like marinara sauce that had just been poured out from a jar. They brought a spoon for my soup, but no fork for the meatballs. I was told that I had to go get my own fork from the self-serve area. We waited another 15 minutes for my husband's panini, then decided to take the cold soup back up to the counter. By then I was admittedly hangry and just asked them to cancel the soup and asked about the panini. The cashier said that they were very busy, but actually the place was maybe 50% at most filled. In the meantime, my husband and I shared and finished the tasty but overly salty meatballs. We waited another 15-20 minutes for the panini and finally decided to cancel the rest of the order. Then I had to stand in line again to get my refund. The only reason I gave 2 stars on this rating instead of 1 star, is because the cashier was gracious enough to refund our entire meal. She also apologized. However, needless to say, we will not be returning here, nor will we be recommending this place to any of our neighbors or out-of-town guests.</review>

<username>Katie Crace< /username>< Date>
1546579600552<//Date>
<rating>3<//rating>< Review>
To start a positive note: the food here is SPECTACULAR. I simply cannot praise the food enough. The decor is very beautiful and gives a lovely high-class aura. Its an enjoyable atmosphere. My boyfriend and I got the housemade meatballs as an appetizer and the Margherita and Prosciutto pizza for the meal. The meatballs were fantastic. Tasty and left you wanting a whole bowlful. The pizza is something I'd eat for the rest of my life. The Neapolitan crust is very good, albeit a little difficult to eat. Just fold the slice in half and continue eating the most flavorful pizza you'll ever encounter.
On the negative aspect, our housemade meatballs were $6.95. For two meatballs. We were beyond shocked when the worker served us only two meatballs and even considered leaving at that point. Additionally, with such done-up decor and the like, the restaurant gives a vibe of service to be had. However, you must go up to the counter and food prep area to order everything. You can't even open a tab if you want to just get your drinks first and finish looking at the menu. With such decor and menu items, you'd at least expect someone to come and ask if the food was alright. A hole was certainly left in our experience due to the lack of table service.
The concept is executed well throughout the restaurant, however, no table service is a major downfall. And with all the employees we saw just loitering around, it wouldn't seem so difficult to make them servers.<//Review>

<text>The Bar: This bar and I go way back. This was my old stomping ground back in the day. Located on Euclid, a stand alone building not attached to a strip mall, which is unusual for the type of bars I've been to lately. They calls this #4, but there are only 2. This place has had a face-lift since the last time I was here. The outside looks brand new. The inside, still the same with a few new improvement, including and indoor smoking lounge, which is a nice touch.
The Crowd: Mixed. College, retired, a few bikers...all seemed like good people having a great time.
Service: Outstanding. All 3 poison pusher were very attentive to the patrons.
Prices: $3.50 pints of PBR, $10 pitchers of domestic, $14 for premium, $10 large pizza.
Entertainment: 3 pool tables ($0.75), 4 electronic dart boards, 6 TV's. Tonight, there was a DJ... I skipped out before having to hear that noise.
Restroom: Less than fabulous, nothing too horrible, but no where to spend any more time than you have to. Typical dive bar crap hole with the classic dive bar condom machine.
Bartenders: Heather, Sam and Tatum.
Closing statement: Still a great bar. Looking forward to a return trip in the future.< /text><Pictures>None<//Pictures>< response>
